<script>
function open_login_iframe() {
    jQuery('#user_item .submenu').remove();
    jQuery('#user_item').append("<DIV class='submenu' style='display:block'></DIV>");
    jQuery('#user_item .submenu').append("<DIV id='nlogin_div' style='font-size:24'>Do not try to login from parts.igem.org. Instead, go to <a href='https://old.igem.org/Login.cgi'>old.igem.org/Login</a> to login to the Registry</div>");
    return;
}
function close_login_iframe(){
   jQuery('#user_item .submenu').empty();
   jQuery('#user_item .submenu').append("<DIV style='padding:10px 200px'>Reloading page...</DIV>");
   location.reload();
}
function open_logout_iframe() {
    jQuery('#user_item').unbind('mouseenter mouseleave');
    jQuery('#user_item .submenu').empty();
    jQuery('#user_item .submenu').append("<DIV id='login_div' >Logout from the iGEM Web Sites<a onClick='close_logout_iframe()' class='close' style='color:white;float:right;'>Close</a></div>");
    jQuery('#user_item .submenu').append("<iframe id='nlogin_iframe' src='http://igem.org/Logout' frameborder=0></iframe>");
    return;
}
function close_logout_iframe(){
   jQuery('#user_item .submenu').empty();
   jQuery('#user_item .submenu').append("<DIV style='padding:10px 200px'>Reloading page...</DIV>");
   location.reload();
}
</script>login<script>

<script>
function click_root_cat( name ) {
    jQuery('#site_nav_bottom').load('http://parts.igem.org/aj/cat/root_clicked.cgi?n=' + name);
}
jQuery(window).resize( function() {
    var pageWrapper       = jQuery('#pageWrapper');
    var pageWrapper_width = pageWrapper.width();
    var nav_wrapper   = jQuery('#site_nav_wrapper');
    var nav_box   = jQuery('#site_nav');
    var nav_width = nav_box.width();
    var pile_item = jQuery('#pile_item');
    var window_width = jQuery(window).width();
    var pivot_width = pageWrapper_width + nav_width + 20;
    var nav_wrapper_origin = 985;
    var right_indent = pivot_width - window_width;
    if ( right_indent <= 0 ) {
        nav_wrapper.css('left', nav_wrapper_origin );
        pile_item.css('right',20);
        pile_item.css('left','auto');        
    } else if ( window_width < pageWrapper_width + 10) {
        nav_wrapper.css('left', ( nav_wrapper_origin - nav_width -10 ) );
        pile_item.css('left',928);        
        pile_item.css('right','auto');
    } else {        
        nav_wrapper.css('left', ( nav_wrapper_origin - right_indent ) );
        pile_item.css('right',20);
        pile_item.css('left','auto');        
    }
});</script></div></div><script> jQuery('#site_nav_wrapper').load('http://parts.igem.org/cgi/aj/cat/site_nav.cgi',{t:'CGI::escape(Part:BBa_K4765135:Hard Information)'});</script>

               <div class="submenu"><div id="igem_submenu2" class="intro"><div class="section" style="float-left; width:250px;"><div class="h1">Quick Links</div><a href="http://parts.igem.org">iGEM Registry</a><br><a href="http://igem.org">iGEM.org</a><br><a href="http://2019.igem.org">2019 iGEM Wiki</a><br><a href="http://2018.igem.org">2018 iGEM Wiki</a><br><a href="http://2017.igem.org">2017 iGEM Wiki</a><br><a href="http://igem.org/Previous_IGEM_Competitions">Previous iGEM Competitions</a><br></div><div class="section" style="float:left;"><div class="h1">About iGEM</div><a href="http://igem.org/About">iGEM</a><br><a href="http://parts.igem.org/Help:Synthetic_Biology">Synthetic Biology</a><br><a href="http://parts.igem.org/Help:Philosophy">Our Philosophy</a><br><a href="http://parts.igem.org/Help:Parts">Parts</a><br><a href="http://parts.igem.org/Help:Plasmid_Backbones">Plasmid Backbones</a><br><a href="http://igem.org/Labs">iGEM Labs</a><br><a href="http://igem.org/Contact">Contact</a><br></div><div class="section1" style="float:right;font-size:18px;line-height:24px;font-family:georgia,serif;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;color:#cccccc; width:250px;">The Registry is a continuously growing community collection of genetic parts that can be mixed and matched
    to build synthetic biology devices and systems. The Registry is part of the Synthetic Biology community's
    efforts to make biology easier to engineer. It provides a resource of available genetic parts to iGEM teams
    and labs.</div></div></div>

    function make_url(after_text) {
        var url = jQuery('.new_menu input[name="search_text"]').val();
        if ( after_text ) { url = url + after_text; }
        return encodeURIComponent( url );
    }

    jQuery('.new_menu #site_search').click( function(){
        location.assign('http://www.google.com/search?q=' + make_url(' site:parts.igem.org') );
    } )
    jQuery('.new_menu #igem_search').click( function(){
        location.assign('http://www.google.com/search?q=' + make_url(' site:igem.org') );
    } )

        location.assign('http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=' + make_url() );
    } )
    jQuery('.new_menu #web_search').click( function(){
        location.assign('http://www.google.com/search?q=' + make_url() );
    } )

    } )

        location.assign('http://parts.igem.org/partsdb/uses.cgi?part=' + make_url() );

        location.assign('http://parts.igem.org/partsdb/search_1000.cgi?q=' + make_url() );
    } )

        location.assign('http://parts.igem.org/partsdb/search_text_input.cgi?q=' + make_url() );

        url = url.replace(' ','_');

<script type="text/javascript">
function click_edit(e, name, id)
{    // regularize the previous selection if any
    var h = universalGetById(document, 'hidden_'+name);
    var v = h.value;
    if (v != '')
    {   universalGetById(document, 'regular_'+name+'_'+v).style.display='inline';
        universalGetById(document, 'edit_'+name+'_'+v).style.display='none';
    }

    universalGetById(document, 'regular_'+name+'_'+id).style.display='none';
    universalGetById(document, 'edit_'+name+'_'+id).style.display='inline';
    h.value = id;
}

function click_cancel(e, name, id)
{   universalGetById(document, 'regular_'+name+'_'+id).style.display = 'inline';
    universalGetById(document, 'edit_'+name+'_'+id).style.display = 'none';
    universalGetById(document, 'hidden_'+name).value = '';
}

function click_submit(e, name, id)
{    var h = universalGetById(document, 'hidden_'+name);
     h.value = id;
     universalGetById(document, 'form_'+name).submit();
}

function click_delete(e, name, id)
{   var f = universalGetById(document, 'form_'+name);
    var h = document.createElement('INPUT');
    h.type  = 'hidden';
    h.name  = 'Delete_'+ name;
    h.value = id;
    f.appendChild(h);
    f.submit();
}

function hide(id)
{   var xtd = universalGetById(document, id);
    xtd.style.display='none';
}

function universalGetById(x, id)
{   if (document.getElementById) return (x.getElementById(id));
    if (document.all)            return (x.all[id]);
}
</script>
